deepak.r IP:127.0.0.1 Dt 19-Apr-15 1:57PM :
 SELECT  el.slno as slno,
						el.emp_id,
						e.name,
						date_format(el.posting_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as posting_date,
						el.type,
						date_format(el.start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(el.end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						el.`leave`,
						el.description,
						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M421/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = ''
		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date
------------------------------------------------
SELECT  el.slno as slno,
						el.emp_id,
						e.name,
						date_format(el.posting_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as posting_date,
						el.type,
						date_format(el.start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(el.end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						el.`leave`,
						el.description,
						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M421/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = ''
		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date

		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M421/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = '2015'
		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date

						el.emp_id,
						e.name,

		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date
------------------------------------------------
SELECT  el.slno as slno,
						el.emp_id,
						e.name,
						date_format(el.posting_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as posting_date,
						el.type,
						date_format(el.start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(el.end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						el.`leave`,
						el.description,
						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M419/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = '2015'
		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date

						date_format(el.posting_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as posting_date,
						el.type,
						date_format(el.start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(el.end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						el.`leave`,
						el.description,
						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M419/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = '2015'
		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date

						date_format(start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						`leave`,
						description,
						status
				FROM emp_leave_ledger
				WHERE emp_id = 'M419/2014'
				AND calc_year = '2015'
jega.v IP:127.0.0.1 Dt 20-Apr-15 4:54PM :
 SELECT  el.slno as slno,
						el.emp_id,
						e.name,
						date_format(el.posting_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as posting_date,
						el.type,
						date_format(el.start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(el.end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						el.`leave`,
						el.description,
						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M419/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = '2015'
		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date

jega.v IP:127.0.0.1 Dt 20-Apr-15 4:18PM :
 SELECT  el.slno as slno,
						el.emp_id,
						e.name,
						date_format(el.posting_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as posting_date,
						el.type,
						date_format(el.start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(el.end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						el.`leave`,
						el.description,
						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M419/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = '2015'
		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date

		AND status = 'APPLIED'

						el.emp_id,
						e.name,
						date_format(el.posting_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as posting_date,
						el.type,
						date_format(el.start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(el.end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						el.`leave`,
						el.description,
						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M419/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = '2015'
		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date
------------------------------------------------

						el.emp_id,
						e.name,

jega.v IP:127.0.0.1 Dt 20-Apr-15 9:42PM :
 SELECT  el.slno as slno,
						el.emp_id,
						e.name,
						date_format(el.posting_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as posting_date,
						el.type,
						date_format(el.start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(el.end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						el.`leave`,
						el.description,
						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M419/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = '2015'
		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date
------------------------------------------------

deepak.r IP:127.0.0.1 Dt 21-Apr-15 7:45PM :
 SELECT  el.slno as slno,
						el.emp_id,
						e.name,
						date_format(el.posting_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as posting_date,
						el.type,
						date_format(el.start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(el.end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						el.`leave`,
						el.description,
						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M421/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = '2015'
		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date

						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M419/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = '2015'

						date_format(el.posting_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as posting_date,
						el.type,
						date_format(el.start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(el.end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						el.`leave`,
						el.description,
						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M419/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = '2015'
		ORDER BY el.emp_id,el.posting_date

 SELECT  el.slno as slno,
						el.emp_id,
						e.name,
						date_format(el.posting_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as posting_date,
						el.type,
						date_format(el.start_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as start_date,
						date_format(el.end_date,'%d-%m-%Y')as end_date,
						el.`leave`,
						el.description,
						el.status
		FROM emp_leave_ledger el
		LEFT JOIN employee e ON el.emp_id = e.id
		WHERE el.approved_by = 'M419/2014'
		AND status = 'APPLIED'
		AND el.calc_year = '2015'
